```jsx
// Fix 1 (R2): rendered-data aggregates across ALL guests (self + others) for Â«Ð¡Ñ‚Ð¾Ð»Â» header
const renderedTableTotal = React.useMemo(() => {
  let total = 0;
  const allGuestIds = [...(myGuestId ? [myGuestId] : []), ...otherGuestIdsFromOrders];
  allGuestIds.forEach((gid) => {
    const orders = ordersByGuestId.get(gid) || [];
    orders.forEach((o) => {
      if ((o.status || '').toLowerCase() !== 'cancelled') {
        total += Number(o.total_amount) || 0;
      }
    });
  });
  return parseFloat(total.toFixed(2));
}, [ordersByGuestId, myGuestId, otherGuestIdsFromOrders]);

// Fix 1 (R2): dish count = sum of item quantities (same semantics as ordersItemCount line 789-792)
const renderedTableDishCount = React.useMemo(() => {
  let count = 0;
  const allGuestIds = [...(myGuestId ? [myGuestId] : []), ...otherGuestIdsFromOrders];
  allGuestIds.forEach((gid) => {
    const orders = ordersByGuestId.get(gid) || [];
    orders.forEach((o) => {
      if ((o.status || '').toLowerCase() === 'cancelled') return;
      const items = itemsByOrder.get(o.id) || [];
      count += items.reduce((s, it) => s + (it.quantity || 1), 0);
    });
  });
  return count;
}, [ordersByGuestId, myGuestId, otherGuestIdsFromOrders, itemsByOrder]);

// Fix 1 (R2): guest count = guests with â‰¥1 non-cancelled order (matches renderedTableTotal filter).
// v7: must NOT count guests with only cancelled orders â€” their total = 0 but header would include
// them in count â†’ "2 Ð³Ð¾ÑÑ‚Ñ Â· 500â‚¸" while one guest has 0â‚¸ (all cancelled). Inconsistent.
// Note: Section 5 Â«Ð—Ð°ÐºÐ°Ð·Ñ‹ ÑÑ‚Ð¾Ð»Ð°Â» still renders ALL orders including cancelled â€” by design,
// this is the service staff-facing view. Only the HEADER counts active guests.
const renderedTableGuestCount = React.useMemo(() => {
  const hasNonCancelled = (gid) =>
    (ordersByGuestId.get(gid) || []).some(
      (o) => (o.status || '').toLowerCase() !== 'cancelled'
    );
  const selfCount = myGuestId && hasNonCancelled(myGuestId) ? 1 : 0;
  const othersCount = otherGuestIdsFromOrders.filter(hasNonCancelled).length;
  return selfCount + othersCount;
}, [myGuestId, ordersByGuestId, otherGuestIdsFromOrders]);

Ð•ÑÐ»Ð¸ Ð² runtime Ð¾Ð±Ð½Ð°Ñ€ÑƒÐ¶Ð¸Ñ‚ÑÑ Ð¸Ð½Ð¾Ðµ Ð¿Ð¾Ð²ÐµÐ´ÐµÐ½Ð¸Ðµ â€” ÑÑ‚Ð¾ Ñ‚Ñ€ÐµÐ±ÑƒÐµÑ‚ Ð¾Ñ‚Ð´ÐµÐ»ÑŒÐ½Ð¾Ð³Ð¾ ÐŸÐ¡Ð¡Ðš, Ð½Ðµ Ð¿Ñ€Ð°Ð²ÐºÐ¸ ÑÑ‚Ð¾Ð³Ð¾.

**Ð¨Ð°Ð³ 2.1** â€” ÐžÐ±Ð½Ð¾Ð²Ð¸Ñ‚ÑŒ `statusBuckets` (ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ð¾ÐºÐ¸ 456-467) Ð´Ð¾Ð±Ð°Ð²Ð»ÐµÐ½Ð¸ÐµÐ¼ `pending_unconfirmed` Ð³Ñ€ÑƒÐ¿Ð¿Ñ‹:

**Ð¢ÐµÐºÑƒÑ‰Ð¸Ð¹ ÐºÐ¾Ð´:**
```jsx
const statusBuckets = React.useMemo(() => {
  const groups = { served: [], in_progress: [] };
  todayMyOrders.forEach(o => {
    const stageInfo = getOrderStatus(o);
    const isServed = stageInfo?.internal_code === 'finish'
      || (!stageInfo?.internal_code && ['served', 'completed'].includes((o.status || '').toLowerCase()));
    const isCancelled = !stageInfo?.internal_code && (o.status || '').toLowerCase() === 'cancelled';
    if (isServed) groups.served.push(o);
    else if (!isCancelled) groups.in_progress.push(o);
  });
  return groups;
}, [todayMyOrders, getOrderStatus]);
```

**Ð—Ð°Ð¼ÐµÐ½Ð¸Ñ‚ÑŒ Ð½Ð°:**
```jsx
const statusBuckets = React.useMemo(() => {
  const groups = { served: [], in_progress: [], pending_unconfirmed: [] };
  todayMyOrders.forEach(o => {
    const stageInfo = getOrderStatus(o);
    const rawStatus = (o.status || '').toLowerCase();
    const isServed = stageInfo?.internal_code === 'finish'
      || (!stageInfo?.internal_code && ['served', 'completed'].includes(rawStatus));
    const isCancelled = !stageInfo?.internal_code && rawStatus === 'cancelled';
    // Fix 2 (R1): pending_unconfirmed = 'submitted' status (awaiting waiter confirmation).
    // Priority: server-side stageInfo wins; only raw status === 'submitted' AND no stage info â†’ pending.
    const isPending = !stageInfo?.internal_code && rawStatus === 'submitted';

    if (isServed) groups.served.push(o);
    else if (isPending) groups.pending_unconfirmed.push(o);
    else if (!isCancelled) groups.in_progress.push(o);
  });
  return groups;
}, [todayMyOrders, getOrderStatus]);
```

**Ð¨Ð°Ð³ 2.2** â€” ÐžÐ±Ð½Ð¾Ð²Ð¸Ñ‚ÑŒ `currentGroupKeys` (ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ð¾ÐºÐ¸ 470-474) Ð´Ð¾Ð±Ð°Ð²Ð»ÐµÐ½Ð¸ÐµÐ¼ ÐºÐ»ÑŽÑ‡Ð° `P`:

  statusBuckets.served.length > 0 ? 'S' : '',
  statusBuckets.in_progress.length > 0 ? 'I' : '',
  cart.length > 0 ? 'C' : ''
].join('');
```

**Ð—Ð°Ð¼ÐµÐ½Ð¸Ñ‚ÑŒ Ð½Ð°:**

  statusBuckets.served.length > 0 ? 'S' : '',
  statusBuckets.in_progress.length > 0 ? 'I' : '',
  statusBuckets.pending_unconfirmed.length > 0 ? 'P' : '', // Fix 2 (R1)
  cart.length > 0 ? 'C' : ''

**Ð—Ð°Ð¼ÐµÐ½Ð¸Ñ‚ÑŒ Ð½Ð°:**

### Ð§Ñ‚Ð¾ Ð½ÑƒÐ¶Ð½Ð¾ ÑÐ´ÐµÐ»Ð°Ñ‚ÑŒ

**Ð¨Ð°Ð³ 3.1** â€” Ð”Ð¾Ð±Ð°Ð²Ð¸Ñ‚ÑŒ durable persist state.

Ð›Ð¾ÐºÐ°Ñ†Ð¸Ñ: Ð²Ð¼ÐµÑÑ‚Ðµ Ñ Ð´Ñ€ÑƒÐ³Ð¸Ð¼Ð¸ useState. Ð’ÑÑ‚Ð°Ð²Ð¸Ñ‚ÑŒ ÐŸÐžÐ¡Ð›Ð• ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ð¾ÐºÐ¸ 114 (`const [showPostRatingEmailSheet, setShowPostRatingEmailSheet] = React.useState(false);`):

> âš ï¸ **v7 fix â€” R4 compliance + consistent identity:** Ð˜ÑÐ¿Ð¾Ð»ÑŒÐ·ÑƒÐµÐ¼ `currentTable?.name ?? currentTable?.code` ÐºÐ°Ðº tableKey â€” **name-first** (ÑÐ¾Ð²Ð¿Ð°Ð´Ð°ÐµÑ‚ Ñ ÑÑƒÑ‰ÐµÑÑ‚Ð²ÑƒÑŽÑ‰ÐµÐ¹ line 385: `name || code || "â€”"`). Ð•ÑÐ»Ð¸ Ð¸ÑÐ¿Ð¾Ð»ÑŒÐ·Ð¾Ð²Ð°Ñ‚ÑŒ code-first, Ð´Ð»Ñ ÑÑ‚Ð¾Ð»Ð° Ñ Ð¾Ð±Ð¾Ð¸Ð¼Ð¸ Ð¿Ð¾Ð»ÑÐ¼Ð¸ ÐºÐ»ÑŽÑ‡ Ñ€Ð°ÑÑ…Ð¾Ð´Ð¸Ð»ÑÑ Ð±Ñ‹ Ñ `rawTableLabel` â†’ Ð¿Ð¾Ð²Ñ‚Ð¾Ñ€Ð½Ñ‹Ð¹ Ð²Ð¸Ð·Ð¸Ñ‚ Ð½Ðµ Ð½Ð°ÑˆÑ‘Ð» Ð±Ñ‹ saved flag. ÐÐ• Ð¸ÑÐ¿Ð¾Ð»ÑŒÐ·Ð¾Ð²Ð°Ñ‚ÑŒ `currentTable?.id` â€” Ð½Ðµ Ð¿Ð¾ÑÐ²Ð»ÑÐµÑ‚ÑÑ Ð² CartView.jsx (grep 0 hits).
>
> R4 FROZEN spec: `cv_terminal_dismissed_{tableId}` â€” per-table ÐºÐ»ÑŽÑ‡, Ð½Ðµ ÐµÐ´Ð¸Ð½ÑÑ‚Ð²ÐµÐ½Ð½Ñ‹Ð¹ Ð³Ð»Ð¾Ð±Ð°Ð»ÑŒÐ½Ñ‹Ð¹ ÐºÐ»ÑŽÑ‡. ÐšÐ°Ð¶Ð´Ñ‹Ð¹ ÑÑ‚Ð¾Ð» Ñ…Ñ€Ð°Ð½Ð¸Ñ‚ Ð½ÐµÐ·Ð°Ð²Ð¸ÑÐ¸Ð¼Ñ‹Ð¹ Ñ„Ð»Ð°Ð³.

```jsx
  // Fix 3 (R4): Per-table durable dismissal.
  // Key: cv_terminal_dismissed_{tableKey} â€” one flag per table (R4 FROZEN spec).
  // tableKey = name ?? code â€” name-first, matching existing line 385 precedence (name || code || "â€”").
  // Using code-first would split terminal state from existing rawTableLabel identity (v7 fix).
  // NOT .id (unverified â€” 0 greps in CartView.jsx).
  const currentTableKey = currentTable?.name ?? currentTable?.code ?? null;

  const [terminalDismissed, setTerminalDismissed] = React.useState(() => {
    if (!currentTableKey || typeof localStorage === 'undefined') return false;
    try {
      return !!localStorage.getItem(`cv_terminal_dismissed_${currentTableKey}`);
    } catch { return false; }
  });
```

**Ð¨Ð°Ð³ 3.2** â€” Ð’Ñ‹Ñ‡Ð¸ÑÐ»Ð¸Ñ‚ÑŒ ÑƒÑÐ»Ð¾Ð²Ð¸Ðµ Ð¿Ð¾ÐºÐ°Ð·Ð° terminal Ñ‡ÐµÑ€ÐµÐ· `useMemo`.

**Ð›Ð¾ÐºÐ°Ñ†Ð¸Ñ (MANDATORY grep Ð´Ð»Ñ placement):**

```bash
grep -a -n "const ordersSum = React.useMemo" menuapp-code-review/pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx
```

**ÐžÐ¶Ð¸Ð´Ð°ÐµÐ¼:** Ð¾Ð´Ð¸Ð½ hit Ð½Ð° ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ð¾ÐºÐµ `~490`.

**Ð¢Ð¾Ñ‡Ð½Ð¾Ðµ Ð¼ÐµÑÑ‚Ð¾ Ð²ÑÑ‚Ð°Ð²ÐºÐ¸:** ÐÐ•ÐŸÐžÐ¡Ð Ð•Ð”Ð¡Ð¢Ð’Ð•ÐÐÐž ÐŸÐ•Ð Ð•Ð” `const ordersSum = React.useMemo` (ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ð¾ÐºÐ° ~490) â€” ÑÑ‚Ð¾ ÐŸÐžÐ¡Ð›Ð• Ð²ÑÐµÑ… useState Ð±Ð»Ð¾ÐºÐ¾Ð² (Ð²ÐºÐ»ÑŽÑ‡Ð°Ñ Ð½Ð¾Ð²Ñ‹Ð¹ Ð¸Ð· Ð¨Ð°Ð³ 3.1) Ð¸ ÐŸÐ•Ð Ð•Ð” `ordersSum` useMemo (Ð½Ð¾ ÐŸÐžÐ¡Ð›Ð• `statusBuckets`/`currentGroupKeys` useMemo Ð½Ð° lines 456-474 â€” Ð¾Ð½Ð¸ Ð¾ÑÑ‚Ð°ÑŽÑ‚ÑÑ Ð²Ñ‹ÑˆÐµ). Ð¢Ð°ÐºÐ¾Ð¹ Ð¿Ð¾Ñ€ÑÐ´Ð¾Ðº Ð³Ð°Ñ€Ð°Ð½Ñ‚Ð¸Ñ€ÑƒÐµÑ‚:

1. **Rules of Hooks ÑÑ‚Ð°Ð±Ð¸Ð»ÐµÐ½**: `tableIsClosed` useMemo Ð²Ñ‹Ð·Ñ‹Ð²Ð°ÐµÑ‚ÑÑ Ð½Ð° ÐºÐ°Ð¶Ð´Ð¾Ð¼ Ñ€ÐµÐ½Ð´ÐµÑ€Ðµ Ð² Ñ„Ð¸ÐºÑÐ¸Ñ€Ð¾Ð²Ð°Ð½Ð½Ð¾Ð¹ Ð¿Ð¾Ð·Ð¸Ñ†Ð¸Ð¸ (Ð¿Ð¾ÑÐ»Ðµ Ð²ÑÐµÑ… useState, Ð¿ÐµÑ€ÐµÐ´ Ð²ÑÐµÐ¼Ð¸ Ð¾ÑÑ‚Ð°Ð»ÑŒÐ½Ñ‹Ð¼Ð¸ useMemo) â†’ Ð½ÐµÑ‚ TDZ crash, Ð½ÐµÑ‚ React warning Â«Rendered more hooks than previous renderÂ».
2. **Dependencies Ð´Ð¾ÑÑ‚ÑƒÐ¿Ð½Ñ‹**: `sessionOrders` â€” ÑÑ‚Ð¾ prop (line 59), ÑƒÐ¶Ðµ Ð² scope; `currentTableKey` â€” derived value Ð½Ð¸Ð¶Ðµ (Ð½Ðµ hook), Ð½Ðµ Ð·Ð°Ð²Ð¸ÑÐ¸Ñ‚ Ð¾Ñ‚ placement.

âš ï¸ **ÐÐ•** Ð²ÑÑ‚Ð°Ð²Ð»ÑÑ‚ÑŒ ÐŸÐžÐ¡Ð›Ð• `ordersSum` Ð¸Ð»Ð¸ ÐŸÐžÐ¡Ð›Ð• Ð´Ñ€ÑƒÐ³Ð¸Ñ… useMemo â€” ÑÑ‚Ð¾ Ð¸Ð·Ð¼ÐµÐ½Ð¸Ñ‚ Ð¿Ð¾Ñ€ÑÐ´Ð¾Ðº hooks Ð¾Ñ‚Ð½Ð¾ÑÐ¸Ñ‚ÐµÐ»ÑŒÐ½Ð¾ ÑÑƒÑ‰ÐµÑÑ‚Ð²ÑƒÑŽÑ‰ÐµÐ³Ð¾ ÐºÐ¾Ð´Ð°, Ñ‡Ñ‚Ð¾ Ð¼Ð¾Ð¶ÐµÑ‚ ÑÐ»Ð¾Ð¼Ð°Ñ‚ÑŒ hooks ordering (ÐµÑÐ»Ð¸ Fix 3 ÐºÐ¾Ð³Ð´Ð°-Ñ‚Ð¾ Ð±ÑƒÐ´ÐµÑ‚ ÑƒÑÐ»Ð¾Ð²Ð½Ð¾ Ð¾Ñ‚ÐºÐ»ÑŽÑ‡Ñ‘Ð½).

```jsx
  // Fix 3 (R4): Table is closed when session has orders AND all non-cancelled orders are 'closed'.
  // (SOM staff invokes closeSession â€” active orders get status='closed' atomically, S286 Ð‘1.)
  // 'cancelled' orders are excluded from the predicate so pre-close cancellations
  // don't prevent the Terminal from showing (v6 fix: handles mixed closed+cancelled sessions).
  const tableIsClosed = React.useMemo(() => {
    if (!Array.isArray(sessionOrders) || sessionOrders.length === 0) return false;
    const nonCancelled = sessionOrders.filter(
      (o) => (o.status || '').toLowerCase() !== 'cancelled'
    );
    // If only cancelled orders exist (edge case) â†’ don't show terminal (no real session activity).
    if (nonCancelled.length === 0) return false;
    return nonCancelled.every((o) => (o.status || '').toLowerCase() === 'closed');
  }, [sessionOrders]);

  // currentTableKey defined in Ð¨Ð°Ð³ 3.1 above (currentTable?.code ?? currentTable?.name ?? null)
  // Do NOT redefine it here â€” it is already declared as const above.
  const showTerminal = tableIsClosed && !!currentTableKey && !terminalDismissed;
```

> âš ï¸ Reviewer: `currentTableKey` Ð¸ `showTerminal` â€” **Ð¾Ð±Ñ‹Ñ‡Ð½Ñ‹Ðµ derived values** (Ð½Ðµ hooks), Ð²Ñ‹Ñ‡Ð¸ÑÐ»ÑÑŽÑ‚ÑÑ ÐºÐ°Ð¶Ð´Ñ‹Ð¹ Ñ€ÐµÐ½Ð´ÐµÑ€. `tableIsClosed` â€” `useMemo`, Ñ‡Ñ‚Ð¾Ð±Ñ‹ Ð½Ðµ Ð¿ÐµÑ€ÐµÑÑ‡Ð¸Ñ‚Ñ‹Ð²Ð°Ñ‚ÑŒ `.every()` Ð¿Ñ€Ð¸ ÐºÐ°Ð¶Ð´Ð¾Ð¼ Ñ€ÐµÐ½Ð´ÐµÑ€Ðµ.

**Ð¨Ð°Ð³ 3.3** â€” Ð ÐµÐ½Ð´ÐµÑ€ Terminal screen Ñ‡ÐµÑ€ÐµÐ· **early return** (Ð±ÐµÐ·Ð¾Ð¿Ð°ÑÐ½Ð¾: Ð²ÑÐµ hooks ÑƒÐ¶Ðµ Ð²Ñ‹Ð·Ð²Ð°Ð½Ñ‹ Ð²Ñ‹ÑˆÐµ).

   9: function lightenColor(hex, amount) {
  10:   const num = parseInt(hex.replace('#', ''), 16);
  11:   const r = Math.min(255, (num >> 16) + Math.round((255 - (num >> 16)) * amount));
  12:   const g = Math.min(255, ((num >> 8) & 0x00FF) + Math.round((255 - ((num >> 8) & 0x00FF)) * amount));
  13:   const b = Math.min(255, (num & 0x0000FF) + Math.round((255 - (num & 0x0000FF)) * amount));
  14:   return `#${(r << 16 | g << 8 | b).toString(16).padStart(6, '0')}`;
  15: }

 281:   // Safe translation with fallback
 282:   const tr = (key, fallback) => {
 283:     const val = typeof t === "function" ? t(key) : "";
 284:     if (!val || typeof val !== "string") return fallback;
 285:     const norm = val.trim();
 286:     if (norm === key || norm.startsWith(key + ":")) return fallback;
 287:     return norm;
 288:   };
 289: 
 290:   // Translation with params
 291:   const trFormat = (key, params, fallback) => {
 292:     const val = typeof t === "function" ? t(key, params) : "";
 293:     if (!val || typeof val !== "string") return fallback;
 294:     const norm = val.trim();
 295:     if (norm === key || norm.startsWith(key)) return fallback;
 296:     return norm;
 297:   };
 298: 
 299:   const pluralizeRu = (n, one, few, many) => {
 300:     const abs = Math.abs(n);
 301:     const m10 = abs % 10;
 302:     const m100 = abs % 100;
 303:     if (m10 === 1 && m100 !== 11) return one;
 304:     if (m10 >= 2 && m10 <= 4 && (m100 < 12 || m100 > 14)) return few;
 305:     return many;
 306:   };
 307:

 312:     }
 313: 
 314:     const code = status.internal_code;
 315:     if (code === 'ready' || code === 'prepared' || code === 'in_progress' || code === 'accepted' || code === 'new') {
 316:       return { label: tr('cart.group.in_progress', 'В работе'), icon: '⏳', color: '#64748b' };
 317:     }
 318:     if (code === 'served' || code === 'delivered' || code === 'finish') {
 319:       return { label: tr('cart.group.served', 'Выдано'), icon: '✓', color: '#059669' };
 320:     }

 752:   // Fix 3 (R4): Table is closed when session has orders AND all non-cancelled orders are 'closed'.
 753:   // (SOM staff invokes closeSession — active orders get status='closed' atomically, S286 Б1.)
 754:   // 'cancelled' orders are excluded from the predicate so pre-close cancellations
 755:   // don't prevent the Terminal from showing (v6 fix: handles mixed closed+cancelled sessions).
 756:   const tableIsClosed = React.useMemo(() => {
 757:     if (!Array.isArray(sessionOrders) || sessionOrders.length === 0) return false;
 758:     const nonCancelled = sessionOrders.filter(
 759:       (o) => (o.status || '').toLowerCase() !== 'cancelled'
 760:     );
 761:     // If only cancelled orders exist (edge case) → don't show terminal (no real session activity).

 763:     return nonCancelled.every((o) => (o.status || '').toLowerCase() === 'closed');
 764:   }, [sessionOrders]);

 836: 
 837: ```jsx
 838:   // Fix 3 (R4): Re-sync dismissal flag when table changes.
 839:   React.useEffect(() => {
 840:     if (!currentTableKey || typeof localStorage === 'undefined') {
 841:       setTerminalDismissed(false);
 842:       return;
 843:     }
 844:     try {
 845:       setTerminalDismissed(!!localStorage.getItem(`cv_terminal_dismissed_${currentTableKey}`));
 846:     } catch {
 847:       setTerminalDismissed(false);
 848:     }
 849:   }, [currentTableKey]); // runs when table changes
 850: ```
 851: 
 852: Это гарантирует: при возврате на ранее dismissed стол — terminal не показывается; при переходе на новый стол — terminal показывается если тот стол закрыт.
 853: 
 854: **НЕ нужно** очищать localStorage (per-table ключи хранятся долго — это и есть «durable persist» по R4).
 855: 
 856: **НЕ делать:**
 857: - ❌ Не использовать `currentTable?.status` — это поле не verified.
 858: - ❌ Не добавлять `tableSession` prop — нарушает scope lock.
 859: - ❌ Не показывать terminal и основной контент одновременно (early return делает это невозможным — это правильно).
 860: - ❌ Не добавлять счётчик обратного отсчёта (не в скоупе).
 861: - ❌ Не удалять основной `return (...)` блок — он должен оставаться после early return.

 233: 
 234: **Проблема:** Header использует `submittedTableTotal` (агрегат из строк 525-531) вместо суммы реально отрендеренных блюд. Нет атрибуции «Вы:»/«Стол:». [CV-NEW-01]

 247: 
 248: ```jsx
 249: {/* CV-50: Dish count + total sum in drawer header (orders + cart) */}
 250: {(ordersSum > 0 || cart.length > 0 || (cartTab === 'table' && submittedTableTotal > 0)) && (() => {
 251:   const ordersItemCount = todayMyOrders.reduce((sum, o) => {
 252:     const items = itemsByOrder.get(o.id) || [];
 253:     return sum + items.reduce((s, it) => s + (it.quantity || 1), 0);
 254:   }, 0);
 255:   const cartItemCount = cart.reduce((sum, item) => sum + (item.quantity || 1), 0);

 257:   const headerTotal = ordersSum + (Number(cartTotalAmount) || 0);

 259:     ? (

 262:       </div>
 263:     )
 264:     : totalDishCount > 0 ? (
 265:       <div className="text-xs text-slate-500 mt-0.5">
 266:         {totalDishCount} {pluralizeRu(totalDishCount, tr('cart.header.dish_one', 'блюдо'), tr('cart.header.dish_few', 'блюда'), tr('cart.header.dish_many', 'блюд'))} · {formatPrice(parseFloat(headerTotal.toFixed(2)))}
 267:       </div>
 268:     ) : null;
 269: })()}

 272: ### Что нужно сделать
 273: 
 274: **Шаг 1.1** — Добавить 3 `useMemo` для rendered-data агрегатов.
 275: 
 276: Локация: сразу ПОСЛЕ `tableOrdersTotal` useMemo (строка 514-523) и ДО `submittedTableTotal` (строка 525). Т.е. новый блок вставляется между строками 523 и 525.
 277: 
 278: Вставить:
 279: 
 280: ```jsx
 281: // Fix 1 (R2): rendered-data aggregates across ALL guests (self + others) for «Стол» header
 282: const renderedTableTotal = React.useMemo(() => {
 283:   let total = 0;
 284:   const allGuestIds = [...(myGuestId ? [myGuestId] : []), ...otherGuestIdsFromOrders];
 285:   allGuestIds.forEach((gid) => {
 286:     const orders = ordersByGuestId.get(gid) || [];
 287:     orders.forEach((o) => {
 288:       if ((o.status || '').toLowerCase() !== 'cancelled') {
 289:         total += Number(o.total_amount) || 0;
 290:       }
 291:     });
 292:   });
 293:   return parseFloat(total.toFixed(2));
 294: }, [ordersByGuestId, myGuestId, otherGuestIdsFromOrders]);
 295: 
 296: // Fix 1 (R2): dish count = sum of item quantities (same semantics as ordersItemCount line 789-792)
 297: const renderedTableDishCount = React.useMemo(() => {
 298:   let count = 0;
 299:   const allGuestIds = [...(myGuestId ? [myGuestId] : []), ...otherGuestIdsFromOrders];
 300:   allGuestIds.forEach((gid) => {
 301:     const orders = ordersByGuestId.get(gid) || [];
 302:     orders.forEach((o) => {
 303:       if ((o.status || '').toLowerCase() === 'cancelled') return;
 304:       const items = itemsByOrder.get(o.id) || [];
 305:       count += items.reduce((s, it) => s + (it.quantity || 1), 0);
 306:     });
 307:   });
 308:   return count;
 309: }, [ordersByGuestId, myGuestId, otherGuestIdsFromOrders, itemsByOrder]);
 310: 
 311: // Fix 1 (R2): guest count = guests with ≥1 non-cancelled order (matches renderedTableTotal filter).
 312: // v7: must NOT count guests with only cancelled orders — their total = 0 but header would include
 313: // them in count → "2 гостя · 500₸" while one guest has 0₸ (all cancelled). Inconsistent.
 314: // Note: Section 5 «Заказы стола» still renders ALL orders including cancelled — by design,
 315: // this is the service staff-facing view. Only the HEADER counts active guests.
 316: const renderedTableGuestCount = React.useMemo(() => {
 317:   const hasNonCancelled = (gid) =>
 318:     (ordersByGuestId.get(gid) || []).some(
 319:       (o) => (o.status || '').toLowerCase() !== 'cancelled'
 320:     );
 321:   const selfCount = myGuestId && hasNonCancelled(myGuestId) ? 1 : 0;
 322:   const othersCount = otherGuestIdsFromOrders.filter(hasNonCancelled).length;
 323:   return selfCount + othersCount;
 324: }, [myGuestId, ordersByGuestId, otherGuestIdsFromOrders]);
 325: ```
 326:

 328: > - `myGuestId` (line 508), `ordersByGuestId` (line 496), `otherGuestIdsFromOrders` (line 510), `itemsByOrder` (prop line 53). Все существуют.

 417: ```
 418: Ожидаем (первый grep):
 419: - `line 456-467`: `statusBuckets` useMemo с `groups = { served: [], in_progress: [] }` — 2 группы, нет pending
 420: - `line 470-474`: `currentGroupKeys` — массив ключей `S`/`I`/`C` (served/in_progress/cart)

 423:

 427: 
 428: ### Архитектура рендера (важно понять перед ревью)
 429: 
 430: Текущая архитектура в блоке State B (обычный режим) — lines 1004-1071:
 431: ```jsx
 432: const bucketOrder = ['served', 'in_progress'];
 433: return bucketOrder.map(key => {
 434:   const orders = statusBuckets[key];
 435:   if (orders.length === 0) return null;
 436:   const isExpanded = !!expandedStatuses[key];
 437:   const isServed = key === 'served';
 438:   // ... <Card>...</Card>
 439: });
 440: ```
 441: 
 442: Это — **динамический рендер через `.map()`**. Fix 2 расширяет `bucketOrder` новым ключом и `statusBuckets` новой группой. Статический JSX-блок добавлять **НЕ НУЖНО**.

 444: ### Что нужно сделать
 445: 
 446: **Шаг 2.0 (Pre-flight verify)** — подтвердить что статус `'submitted'` реально используется в заказах:
 447: 
 448: ```bash
 449: grep -a -n "'submitted'" menuapp-code-review/pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx
 450: ```
 451: 
 452: **Ожидаем:** ≥1 hit. На verify reference: line 528 (`o.status === 'submitted'` в filter для `submittedTableTotal`). Это подтверждает что `submitted` — легитимное значение `order.status` в этом коде → Fix 2 маппинг `rawStatus === 'submitted'` корректен.
 453: 
 454: Если grep возвращает 0 hits — **ОСТАНОВИТЬСЯ**, сообщить Cowork: «статус `'submitted'` не найден в CartView.jsx, маппинг Fix 2 может быть неверным».
 455: 
 456: **Шаг 2.0b (Assumption — не verifiable через grep)** — `getOrderStatus` является prop (line 54), его runtime-поведение не видно из CartView.jsx.
 457: 
 458: ```bash
 459: grep -a -n "getOrderStatus" menuapp-code-review/pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx | head -5
 460: ```
 461: **Ожидаем:** `line 54` — prop definition. Строки вызова: `getOrderStatus(o)` в statusBuckets и рендер-блоках.
 462: 
 463: > **ASSUMPTION (проверить вручную в runtime):** `getOrderStatus(submittedOrder)?.internal_code` = falsy пока официант не принял заказ в SOM. После принятия — `internal_code` становится непустым → `isPending = false` → заказ уходит в `in_progress` bucket. Это design decision: сервер-сигнал приоритетнее raw status.
 464: >
 465: > Fix 2 реализует это правильно: `statusBuckets` использует `isPending = !stageInfo?.internal_code && rawStatus === 'submitted'`. Badge в Шаг 2.6 использует ТОТ ЖЕ guard (v7 fix). Если в runtime обнаружится иное поведение — это требует отдельного ПССК, не правки этого.
 466: 
 467: **Шаг 2.1** — Обновить `statusBuckets` (строки 456-467) добавлением `pending_unconfirmed` группы:
 468: 
 469: **Текущий код:**
 470: ```jsx
 471: const statusBuckets = React.useMemo(() => {
 472:   const groups = { served: [], in_progress: [] };
 473:   todayMyOrders.forEach(o => {
 474:     const stageInfo = getOrderStatus(o);
 475:     const isServed = stageInfo?.internal_code === 'finish'
 476:       || (!stageInfo?.internal_code && ['served', 'completed'].includes((o.status || '').toLowerCase()));
 477:     const isCancelled = !stageInfo?.internal_code && (o.status || '').toLowerCase() === 'cancelled';
 478:     if (isServed) groups.served.push(o);
 479:     else if (!isCancelled) groups.in_progress.push(o);
 480:   });
 481:   return groups;
 482: }, [todayMyOrders, getOrderStatus]);
 483: ```
 484: 
 485: **Заменить на:**
 486: ```jsx
 487: const statusBuckets = React.useMemo(() => {
 488:   const groups = { served: [], in_progress: [], pending_unconfirmed: [] };
 489:   todayMyOrders.forEach(o => {
 490:     const stageInfo = getOrderStatus(o);
 491:     const rawStatus = (o.status || '').toLowerCase();
 492:     const isServed = stageInfo?.internal_code === 'finish'
 493:       || (!stageInfo?.internal_code && ['served', 'completed'].includes(rawStatus));
 494:     const isCancelled = !stageInfo?.internal_code && rawStatus === 'cancelled';
 495:     // Fix 2 (R1): pending_unconfirmed = 'submitted' status (awaiting waiter confirmation).
 496:     // Priority: server-side stageInfo wins; only raw status === 'submitted' AND no stage info → pending.
 497:     const isPending = !stageInfo?.internal_code && rawStatus === 'submitted';
 498: 
 499:     if (isServed) groups.served.push(o);
 500:     else if (isPending) groups.pending_unconfirmed.push(o);
 501:     else if (!isCancelled) groups.in_progress.push(o);
 502:   });
 503:   return groups;
 504: }, [todayMyOrders, getOrderStatus]);
 505: ```

# Codex Reviewer Findings — ПССК Prompt Quality Review
Chain: pssk-cv-b2-260416-v7-260416-200025-792a

## Issues Found
1. [CRITICAL] Fix 2 misses the `isV8` special-render branch — the prompt updates only `statusBuckets`, `currentGroupKeys`, `bucketDisplayNames`, `bucketOrder`, and the table-item badge, but it never updates the separate branch at `pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx:927-1005`. After applying the prompt, a session with `served > 0`, `pending_unconfirmed > 0`, `in_progress === 0`, and empty cart still hits “Ничего не ждёте” and hides the new pending bucket. PROMPT FIX: add a mandatory step in Fix 2 to gate `isV8` with `statusBuckets.pending_unconfirmed.length === 0`, or render the pending bucket inside that branch.
2. [CRITICAL] Fix order conflicts with Fix 2 preflight verification — the prompt mandates `Fix 1 → Fix 2`, but Fix 1 Step 1.3 deletes `submittedTableTotal` at `pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx:525-531`, and the only literal `'submitted'` hit in the current file is at line 528. Fix 2 Step 2.0 then tells the executor to grep `'submitted'` and stop if it gets 0 hits. Following the prompt in order can therefore trigger a false stop. PROMPT FIX: move the `'submitted'` verification into the shared Preparation block before Fix 1, or rewrite Step 2.0 as a pre-Fix1 snapshot assumption instead of a live post-Fix1 gate.
3. [MEDIUM] Fix 3 contradicts itself on `currentTableKey` precedence — the prompt summary and Step 3.1/snippet use `currentTable?.name ?? currentTable?.code ?? null` to match `pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx:385`, but Step 3.2 commentary and Acceptance Criteria require `currentTable?.code ?? currentTable?.name ?? null`. That ambiguity affects localStorage identity and can make a correct implementation fail review. PROMPT FIX: normalize every prose snippet, code comment, and acceptance check to one order; based on line 385, `name ?? code` is the consistent choice.
4. [MEDIUM] Fix 1 and Fix 4 use a weaker cancelled-order predicate than the file already uses — the prompt excludes cancelled orders with raw `o.status === 'cancelled'`, while existing code already normalizes cancellation through `getOrderStatus()` plus raw fallback at `pages/PublicMenu/CartView.jsx:443-446` and `459-463`. If runtime cancellation is exposed only through `internal_code`, the new header/self totals can drift from the rest of the UI. PROMPT FIX: reuse the existing normalized cancellation predicate in `renderedTableTotal`, `renderedTableGuestCount`, and `selfTotal`, or explicitly label raw-status-only behavior as an assumption.
5. [LOW] Mandatory visual QA is underspecified — the prompt requires “Verify at 375px width” and several layout assertions, but it does not provide a browser procedure, a viewport tool, or a fallback rule for non-visual runners. That invites unverified claims of completion. PROMPT FIX: either provide the exact browser/preview workflow to use, or relabel the mobile-first section as manual QA follow-up rather than mandatory executor verification.

## Summary
Total: 5 issues (2 CRITICAL, 2 MEDIUM, 1 LOW)

## Additional Risks
- The wrapper assumes a `Write` tool and writable `pipeline/*` paths. In this runner, edits outside the worktree were blocked, so delivery can fail operationally even when the review itself is complete.
- Fix 2 also relies on runtime behavior of `getOrderStatus(submittedOrder)` without an inline contract. The prompt partly labels this as an assumption, but the resulting UX still depends on external behavior not fully inlined here.

## Prompt Clarity
- Overall clarity: 3/5
- What was most clear: the scope lock to `CartView.jsx`, the verified identifier checks, and the concrete replacement snippets for each fix.
- What was ambiguous or could cause hesitation: the cross-fix dependency between Fix 1 and Fix 2, the contradictory `currentTableKey` order in Fix 3, and the missing handling of the `isV8` branch for pending orders.
- Missing context: how to verify mobile layout in-runner, whether cancellation may arrive only via `internal_code`, and whether the executor is guaranteed access to the required pipeline write paths/tools.
